   1              	# 1 "src/boot/SmartStart32.S"
   1              	﻿;@"+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++"
   0              	
   0              	
   2              	;@"																			"
   3              	;@"      Filename: smartstart32.s											"
   4              	;@"      Copyright(c): Leon de Boer(LdB) 2017								"
   5              	;@"      Version: 2.02														"
   6              	;@"																			"
   7              	;@"**************[ THIS CODE IS FREEWARE UNDER CC Attribution]**************"
   8              	;@"																            "
   9              	;@"     This sourcecode is released for the purpose to promote programming  "
  10              	;@"  on the Raspberry Pi. You may redistribute it and/or modify with the    "
  11              	;@"  following disclaimer and condition.                                    "
  12              	;@"																            "
  13              	;@"      The SOURCE CODE is distributed "AS IS" WITHOUT WARRANTIES AS TO    "
  14              	;@"   PERFORMANCE OF MERCHANTABILITY WHETHER EXPRESSED OR IMPLIED.          "
  15              	;@"   Redistributions of source code must retain the copyright notices to   "
  16              	;@"   maintain the author credit (attribution) .							"
  17              	;@"																			"
  18              	;@"*************************************************************************"
  19              	;@"                                                                         "
  20              	;@"       This code expands on my earlier SmartStart bootstub assembler for "
  21              	;@" the Pi 1/2/3. It simplifies some of the autodetect code but importantly "
  22              	;@" directly supports multicore operation in C/C++. To do that it provides  "
  23              	;@" stack space to each core and provides a modified bootloader spinlock    "
  24              	;@" that protects against registers R0-R3 trashed. As any C/C++ compiler    "
  25              	;@" code will trash those registers, to use C/C++ in multicore programming  "
  26              	;@" this protection must be done.											"
  27              	;@"      The downside is this bootstub must be a little more complex in     "
  28              	;@" that it must start and setup multiple cores. The code is much more      "
  29              	;@" connected to the linker file which provides memory space to each core.  "
  30              	;@"       There is however matching paired AARCH64 stub and linker files    "
  31              	;@" so code written for this setup can be ported to AARCH64 with ease.		"
  32              	;@"																            "
  33              	;@"+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++"
  34              	
  35              	;@"========================================================================="
  36              	;@"				 	 ARM CPU ID CONSTANT DEFINITIONS					    "
  37              	;@"========================================================================="
  38              	.equ ARM6_CPU_ID, 0x410FB767					;@ CPU id a BCM2835 reports
  39              	.equ ARM7_CPU_ID, 0x410FC073					;@ CPU id a BCM2836 reports
  40              	.equ ARM8_CPU_ID, 0x410FD034					;@ CPU id a BCM2837 reports
  41              	
  42              	;@"========================================================================="
  43              	;@"				 	 ARM CPU MODE CONSTANT DEFINITIONS					    "
  44              	;@"========================================================================="
  45              	.equ CPU_FIQMODE, 0x11							;@ CPU in FIQ mode
  46              	.equ CPU_IRQMODE, 0x12							;@ CPU in IRQ mode
  47              	.equ CPU_SVCMODE, 0x13							;@ CPU in SVC mode
  48              	.equ CPU_HYPMODE, 0x1A							;@ CPU in HYP mode
  49              	
  50              	;@"========================================================================="
  51              	;@"				 ARM CPU IRQ/FIQ BIT CONSTANT DEFINITIONS				    "
  52              	;@"========================================================================="
  53              	#define I_Bit  (1 << 7)							// Irq flag bit in cpsr (CPUMODE register)
  54              	#define F_Bit  (1 << 6)							// Fiq flag bit in cpsr (CPUMODE register)
ARM GAS  C:\Users\Carlo\AppData\Local\Temp\cc4uwfQk.s 			page 2


  55              	
  56              	;@"========================================================================="
  57              	;@"				 	 ARM CPU MODE CONSTANT DEFINITIONS					    "
  58              	;@"========================================================================="
  59              	.equ CPU_FIQMODE_VALUE, (CPU_FIQMODE | I_Bit | F_Bit)	;@ CPU in FIQ mode with irq, fiq off
  60              	.equ CPU_IRQMODE_VALUE, (CPU_IRQMODE | I_Bit | F_Bit)	;@ CPU in IRQ mode with irq, fiq off
  61              	.equ CPU_SVCMODE_VALUE, (CPU_SVCMODE | I_Bit | F_Bit)	;@ CPU in SVC mode with irq, fiq off
  62              	
  63              	;@"*************************************************************************"
  64              	;@"          INTERNAL DATA FOR SMARTSTART NOT EXPOSED TO INTERFACE			"
  65              	;@"*************************************************************************"
  66              	.section ".data.smartstart", "aw"
  67              	.balign 4
  68              	
  69 0000 00000000 	RPi_BusAlias	: .4byte 0;				// Address offset between VC4 physical address and ARM address needed f
  70              	
  71              	
  72              	
  73              	.globl RPi_CPUCurrentMode;				// Make sure RPi_CPUCurrentMode label is global
  74 0004 00000000 	RPi_CPUCurrentMode : .4byte 0;			//  CPU current Mode is 4 byte variable
  75              	
  76              	.globl RPi_Heap; @ Make sure RPi_Heap label is global
  77 0008 00000000 	RPi_Heap : .4byte 0; @ RPi_Heap is 4 byte variable
  78              	
  79              	.section ".text.startup", "ax", %progbits
  80              	.balign	4
  81              	.globl _start
  82              	.syntax unified
  83              	.arm
  84              	_start:
  85              	;@"================================================================"
  86              	;@ Grab cpu mode and start address and hold in a high register.
  87              	;@"================================================================"
  88 0000 0FC0A0E1 		mov r12, pc;							;@ Hold boot address in high register R12
  89 0004 00B00FE1 		mrs r11, CPSR							;@ Read current CPU mode
  90 0008 1FB00BE2 		and r11, r11, #0x1F						;@ Clear all but CPU mode bits in register r11
  91              	;@"================================================================"
  92              	;@ If the cpu is in HYP_MODE(EL2) we will bring it SVC_MODE (EL1).
  93              	;@"================================================================"
  94              	multicore_start:
  95 000c 00000FE1 	    mrs r0,cpsr								;@ Fetch the cpsr register which includes CPU mode bits
  96 0010 1F1000E2 	 	and r1, r0, #0x1F						;@ Mask off the CPU mode bits to register r1
  97 0014 1A0051E3 	 	cmp r1, #CPU_HYPMODE					;@ Check we are in HYP_MODE
  98 0018 0500001A 		bne .NotInHypMode						;@ Branch if not equal meaning was not in HYP_MODE
  99 001c 1F00C0E3 		bic r0,r0,#0x1F							;@ Clear the CPU mode bits in register r0
 100 0020 D30080E3 		orr r0, r0, #CPU_SVCMODE_VALUE			;@ SVC_MODE bits onto register with Irq/Fiq disabled
 101 0024 00F06FE1 	    msr spsr_cxsf,r0						;@ Hold value in spsr_cxsf
